<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tokenizer</h3><a id="user-content-tokenizer" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tokenizer" href="#tokenizer"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The following keys are used to describe the tokenizer of the model. It is recommended that model authors support as many of these as possible, as it will allow for better tokenization quality with supported executors.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">GGML</h4><a id="user-content-ggml" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: GGML" href="#ggml"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">GGML supports an embedded vocabulary that enables inference of the model, but implementations of tokenization using this vocabulary (i.e. <code>llama.cpp</code>'s tokenizer) may have lower accuracy than the original tokenizer used for the model. When a more accurate tokenizer is available and supported, it should be used instead.</p>
<p dir="auto">It is not guaranteed to be standardized across models, and may change in the future. It is recommended that model authors use a more standardized tokenizer if possible.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.model: string</code>: The name of the tokenizer model.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>llama</code>: Llama style SentencePiece (tokens and scores extracted from HF <code>tokenizer.model</code>)</li>
<li><code>replit</code>: Replit style SentencePiece (tokens and scores extracted from HF <code>spiece.model</code>)</li>
<li><code>gpt2</code>: GPT-2 / GPT-NeoX style BPE (tokens extracted from HF <code>tokenizer.json</code>)</li>
<li><code>rwkv</code>: RWKV tokenizer</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.tokens: array[string]</code>: A list of tokens indexed by the token ID used by the model.</li>
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.scores: array[float32]</code>: If present, the score/probability of each token. If not present, all tokens are assumed to have equal probability. If present, it must have the same length and index as <code>tokens</code>.</li>
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.token_type: array[int32]</code>: The token type (1=normal, 2=unknown, 3=control, 4=user defined, 5=unused, 6=byte). If present, it must have the same length and index as <code>tokens</code>.</li>
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.merges: array[string]</code>: If present, the merges of the tokenizer. If not present, the tokens are assumed to be atomic.</li>
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.added_tokens: array[string]</code>: If present, tokens that were added after training.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Special tokens</h5><a id="user-content-special-tokens" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Special tokens" href="#special-tokens"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.bos_token_id: uint32</code>: Beginning of sequence marker</li>
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.eos_token_id: uint32</code>: End of sequence marker</li>
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.unknown_token_id: uint32</code>: Unknown token</li>
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.separator_token_id: uint32</code>: Separator token</li>
<li><code>tokenizer.ggml.padding_token_id: uint32</code>: Padding token</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Hugging Face</h4><a id="user-content-hugging-face" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Hugging Face" href="#hugging-face"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Hugging Face maintains their own <code>tokenizers</code> library that supports a wide variety of tokenizers. If your executor uses this library, it may be able to use the model's tokenizer directly.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>tokenizer.huggingface.json: string</code>: the entirety of the HF <code>tokenizer.json</code> for a given model (e.g. <a href="https://huggingface.co/mosaicml/mpt-7b-instruct/blob/main/tokenizer.json" rel="nofollow">https://huggingface.co/mosaicml/mpt-7b-instruct/blob/main/tokenizer.json</a>). Included for compatibility with executors that support HF tokenizers directly.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Other</h4><a id="user-content-other" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Other" href="#other"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Other tokenizers may be used, but are not necessarily standardized. They may be executor-specific. They will be documented here as they are discovered/further developed.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>tokenizer.rwkv.world: string</code>: a RWKV World tokenizer, like <a href="https://github.com/BlinkDL/ChatRWKV/blob/main/tokenizer/rwkv_vocab_v20230424.txt">this</a>. This text file should be included verbatim.</li>
<li><code>tokenizer.chat_template : string</code>: a Jinja template that specifies the input format expected by the model. For more details see: <a href="https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/main/en/chat_templating" rel="nofollow">https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/main/en/chat_templating</a></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Computation graph</h3><a id="user-content-computation-graph" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Computation graph" href="#computation-graph"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This is a future extension and still needs to be discussed, and may necessitate a new GGUF version. At the time of writing, the primary blocker is the stabilization of the computation graph format.</p>
<p dir="auto">A sample computation graph of GGML nodes could be included in the model itself, allowing an executor to run the model without providing its own implementation of the architecture. This would allow for a more consistent experience across executors, and would allow for more complex architectures to be supported without requiring the executor to implement them.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Standardized tensor names</h2><a id="user-content-standardized-tensor-names" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Standardized tensor names" href="#standardized-tensor-names"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To minimize complexity and maximize compatibility, it is recommended that models using the transformer architecture use the following naming convention for their tensors:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Base layers</h3><a id="user-content-base-layers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Base layers" href="#base-layers"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>AA.weight</code> <code>AA.bias</code></p>
<p dir="auto">where <code>AA</code> can be:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>token_embd</code>: Token embedding layer</li>
<li><code>pos_embd</code>: Position embedding layer</li>
<li><code>output_norm</code>: Output normalization layer</li>
<li><code>output</code>: Output layer</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Attention and feed-forward layer blocks</h3><a id="user-content-attention-and-feed-forward-layer-blocks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Attention and feed-forward layer blocks" href="#attention-and-feed-forward-layer-blocks"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>blk.N.BB.weight</code> <code>blk.N.BB.bias</code></p>
<p dir="auto">where N signifies the block number a layer belongs to, and where <code>BB</code> could be:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>attn_norm</code>: Attention normalization layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>attn_norm_2</code>: Attention normalization layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>attn_qkv</code>: Attention query-key-value layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>attn_q</code>: Attention query layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>attn_k</code>: Attention key layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>attn_v</code>: Attention value layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>attn_output</code>: Attention output layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ffn_norm</code>: Feed-forward network normalization layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ffn_up</code>: Feed-forward network "up" layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ffn_gate</code>: Feed-forward network "gate" layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ffn_down</code>: Feed-forward network "down" layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ffn_gate_inp</code>: Expert-routing layer for the Feed-forward network in MoE models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ffn_gate_exp</code>: Feed-forward network "gate" layer per expert in MoE models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ffn_down_exp</code>: Feed-forward network "down" layer per expert in MoE models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ffn_up_exp</code>: Feed-forward network "up" layer per expert in MoE models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ssm_in</code>: State space model input projections layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ssm_conv1d</code>: State space model rolling/shift layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ssm_x</code>: State space model selective parametrization layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ssm_a</code>: State space model state compression layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ssm_d</code>: State space model skip connection layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ssm_dt</code>: State space model time step layer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ssm_out</code>: State space model output projection layer</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Version History</h2><a id="user-content-version-history" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Version History" href="#version-history"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This document is actively updated to describe the current state of the metadata, and these changes are not tracked outside of the commits.</p>
<p dir="auto">However, the format <em>itself</em> has changed. The following sections describe the changes to the format itself.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">v3</h3><a id="user-content-v3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: v3" href="#v3"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Adds big-endian support.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">v2</h3><a id="user-content-v2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: v2" href="#v2"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Most countable values (lengths, etc) were changed from <code>uint32</code> to <code>uint64</code> to allow for larger models to be supported in the future.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">v1</h3><a id="user-content-v1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: v1" href="#v1"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Initial version.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Historical State of Affairs</h2><a id="user-content-historical-state-of-affairs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Historical State of Affairs" href="#historical-state-of-affairs"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The following information is provided for context, but is not necessary to understand the rest of this document.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Overview</h3><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Overview" href="#overview"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">At present, there are three GGML file formats floating around for LLMs:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>GGML</strong> (unversioned): baseline format, with no versioning or alignment.</li>
<li><strong>GGMF</strong> (versioned): the same as GGML, but with versioning. Only one version exists.</li>
<li><strong>GGJT</strong>: Aligns the tensors to allow for use with <code>mmap</code>, which requires alignment. v1, v2 and v3 are identical, but the latter versions use a different quantization scheme that is incompatible with previous versions.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">GGML is primarily used by the examples in <code>ggml</code>, while GGJT is used by <code>llama.cpp</code> models. Other executors may use any of the three formats, but this is not 'officially' supported.</p>
<p dir="auto">These formats share the same fundamental structure:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a magic number with an optional version number</li>
<li>model-specific hyperparameters, including
<ul dir="auto">
<li>metadata about the model, such as the number of layers, the number of heads, etc.</li>
<li>a <code>ftype</code> that describes the type of the majority of the tensors,
<ul dir="auto">
<li>for GGML files, the quantization version is encoded in the <code>ftype</code> divided by 1000</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>an embedded vocabulary, which is a list of strings with length prepended. The GGMF/GGJT formats embed a float32 score next to the strings.</li>
<li>finally, a list of tensors with their length-prepended name, type, and (aligned, in the case of GGJT) tensor data</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Notably, this structure does not identify what model architecture the model belongs to, nor does it offer any flexibility for changing the structure of the hyperparameters. This means that the only way to add new hyperparameters is to add them to the end of the list, which is a breaking change for existing models.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Drawbacks</h3><a id="user-content-drawbacks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Drawbacks" href="#drawbacks"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Unfortunately, over the last few months, there are a few issues that have become apparent with the existing models:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There's no way to identify which model architecture a given model is for, because that information isn't present
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Similarly, existing programs cannot intelligently fail upon encountering new architectures</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Adding or removing any new hyperparameters is a breaking change, which is impossible for a reader to detect without using heuristics</li>
<li>Each model architecture requires its own conversion script to their architecture's variant of GGML</li>
<li>Maintaining backwards compatibility without breaking the structure of the format requires clever tricks, like packing the quantization version into the ftype, which are not guaranteed to be picked up by readers/writers, and are not consistent between the two formats</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why not other formats?</h3><a id="user-content-why-not-other-formats" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why not other formats?" href="#why-not-other-formats"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">There are a few other formats that could be used, but issues include:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>requiring additional dependencies to load or save the model, which is complicated in a C environment</li>
<li>limited or no support for 4-bit quantization</li>
<li>existing cultural expectations (e.g. whether or not the model is a directory or a file)</li>
<li>lack of support for embedded vocabularies</li>
<li>lack of control over direction of future development</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Ultimately, it is likely that GGUF will remain necessary for the foreseeable future, and it is better to have a single format that is well-documented and supported by all executors than to contort an existing format to fit the needs of GGML.</p>
</article></div><div class="d-none"></div></section></div></div></div> </div> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ScrollMarksContainer-module__scrollMarksContainer__Eu7uU" id="find-result-marks-container"></div><div class="d-none"></div><div class="d-none"></div></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> <script type="application/json" id="__PRIMER_DATA__R_1___">{"resolvedServerColorMode":"day"}</script></div>
</react-app>




  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>

  </div>
